%%\tagged{Ans@MultiAns, Type@Concept, Topic@Limit, Sub@Continuity, Sub@Disc-Jump, Sub@Piecewise, File@0004}{
\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0004. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
{x^{2} - 2 \, x} & , & x\leq {0}\\
{-x - 1} & , & {0}<x\leq{2}\\
{{\left(x - 2\right)}^{2} - 3} & , & x>{2}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{0}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{0}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{

\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{1}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{1}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

{x^{2} + 2 \, x - 31} & , & x>{5}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{0}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{0}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

{x^{2} - 9} & , & {2}<x\leq{4}\\
{{\left(x - 3\right)}^{2} + 6} & , & x>{4}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{2}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{2}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
{x^{2} - 5 \, x - 21} & , & x\leq {-3}\\
{-x - 1} & , & {-3}<x\leq{1}\\
{x - 3} & , & x>{1}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{-3}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{-3}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0004. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
{x^{2} - 3} & , & x\leq {2}\\
{x^{2} + 3 \, x - 10} & , & {2}<x\leq{6}\\
{x^{2} + 8} & , & x>{6}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{2}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{2}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
{x^{2} + 4 \, x + 34} & , & x\leq {-3}\\
{x^{2} - 5 \, x + 6} & , & {-3}<x\leq{-1}\\
{x + 13} & , & x>{-1}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{-3}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{-3}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

{x^{2} - 3 \, x + 39} & , & x\leq {-3}\\
{x^{2} - 9 \, x + 20} & , & {-3}<x\leq{-1}\\
{x + 31} & , & x>{-1}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{-3}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{-3}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0004. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
{{\left(x - 2\right)}^{2} - 1} & , & x\leq {0}\\
{x + 2} & , & {0}<x\leq{5}\\
{x + 2} & , & x>{5}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{0}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{0}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
{x + 3} & , & x\leq {0}\\
{-x + 2} & , & {0}<x\leq{2}\\
{x^{2} - 4} & , & x>{2}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{0}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{0}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0004. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Let $f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{clc}
{{\left(x + 1\right)}^{2} + 13} & , & x\leq {1}\\
{{\left(x - 5\right)}^{2}} & , & {1}<x\leq{3}\\
{x^{2} - x - 2} & , & x>{3}
\end{array}\right.$.  

Find the numbers at which $f$ is discontinuous: $x=\answer{1}$\\ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

\input{Limit-Concept-0004.HELP.tex}

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the right?\\  $x=\answer{None}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')

At which of these points of discontinuity is $f$ continuous from the left?\\  $x=\answer{1}$ \qquad (If no such numbers exist, enter ``None'')
\end{problem}}%}

\end{array}\right.$.
